Valley Pass The trees of the forest to the west give way abruptly to a low rolling grassland nestled between huge looming mountains. Smelly herd beasts upset the tranquility of the area with their grass-nibbling and farting. The only other disruptions in the billowing grasses are a small adobe hut, and a grove of strange trees nearby. The valley is level with the forest floor to the west, but the eastern wall of the valley is formed by a large plateau rising at least as high as the mountains around it, casting a dark shadow on much of the grassland through much of the day.
